GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - c1*beta*v - omega0**c2*(gamma*t + c3)*x
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed):
\[
0.7193212363\sin(t)\;-\;0.08567815673\,v^3\;-\;1.91960248273\,v\;-\;1.730295313206\,x(0.0808213006269\,t+1)
\]
So GT structure is: **sin(t)** term with constant amplitude; **polynomial in v** containing \(v^3\) and \(v\); and an **x·t cross-term** that is exactly linear in both \(x\) and \(t\): \(-Kx - (K\gamma)xt\). No exponentials, no rational-in-x denominators, no \(\cos\), no \(|v|\), no \(x^2,x^3,x^5\), etc.

Below, for each candidate, I check whether by choosing its constants (and possibly restricting to a plausible continuous domain like \(v\ge 0\)) it can reproduce **exactly**: (i) a pure \(\sin(t)\) term (not \(\sin(\text{affine in }t)\) unless it can be made \(\sin(t)\)); (ii) both \(v^3\) and \(v\) terms with the right independence from \(x,t\); (iii) the \(-x - xt\) linear cross-term (no denominators, no trig modulation, no exponentials).

---

### 1. \(c0 + c1 e^{c2 x} + c3 v|v| + c4 x^3 + c5 v + c6 e^{c7 t}\sin(c8 t+c9)\)
- Has \(v|v|\) (piecewise \(v^2\) with sign), not \(v^3\). No way to get \(v^3\) from \(v|v|\) by constants/domain restriction.
- The \(x\)-dependence is via \(e^{c2 x}\) and \(x^3\), not linear \(x\) and \(xt\).
- Time sinusoid is multiplied by \(e^{c7 t}\); to match GT’s constant-amplitude \(\sin(t)\), need \(c7=0\). Also need \(c8=1, c9=0\) (or phase-equivalent). That part is possible, but the missing \(v^3\) and wrong \(x,t\) coupling kill it.
**No match.**

### 2. \(c0 x/(c1+x)+c2 v+c3 x+c4 e^{c5 t}\sin(c6 t+c7)\)
- No \(v^3\) term.
- No \(xt\) term; only \(x\) and rational \(x/(c1+x)\).
**No match.**

### 3. Like (1) plus \(x^5\)

**No match.**

- No \(xt\) term.
**No match.**

**GT numerical expression:** `-0.0856781567252997*v**3 - 1.91960248272986*v - 1.73029531320599*x*(0.0808213006269486*t + 1) + 0.719321236251799*sin(t)`

Expanding: `-0.0856781567252997*v**3 - 1.91960248272986*v - 1.73029531320599*x*0.0808213006269486*t - 1.73029531320599*x + 0.719321236251799*sin(t)`

So GT = `-0.0857*v**3 - 1.9196*v - 0.1398*x*t - 1.7303*x + 0.7193*sin(t)`

The key basis functions in GT are: **v³, v, x·t, x, sin(t)**

Now let me analyze each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `c0 + c1*exp(c2*x) + c3*v*Abs(v) + c4*x**3 + c5*v + c6*exp(c7*t)*sin(c8*t + c9)`
- Has v*|v| (not v³), exp(x), x³ instead of x·t. v*|v| ≠ v³ since v takes both signs. No x·t term. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 2:** `c0*x/(c1 + x) + c2*v + c3*x + c4*exp(c5*t)*sin(c6*t + c7)`
- Rational function of x, no v³, no x·t. Missing v³ and x·t. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 3:** Similar to 1 with x⁵ added. Same issues. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 4:** Rational functions, no v³, no x·t. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 5:** No v³, no x·t. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 6:** No v³, no x·t. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 7:** Has v*|v| not v³, no x·t. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 8:** `c0*x*cos(c1*t) + c2*x + c3*exp(c4*t)*cos(c5*t + c6)`
- No v terms at all. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 9-15:** Missing v³ or x·t or both. **[NO MATCH]** for all.

**Candidate 16:** Has v*|v| not v³. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 17:** `c0*x/(c1+x²) + c2*v + c3*x*cos(c4*t) + c5*v³ + c6*x³ + c7*exp(c8*t)*cos(c9*t)`
- Has v³, v. Has x*cos(c4*t) - can this give x·t? No, cos is periodic, not linear in t. Has x/(c1+x²) and x³ - extra terms. The x·t term cannot be produced by x*cos(t). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 18-42:** Let me check each for the required basis {v³, v, x·t, x, sin(t)}.

**Candidate 43:** `c0*x/(c1+x²) + c2*v*x² + c3*v³ + c4*v + c5*x³ + c6*x*cos(c7*t) + c8*x + c9*v`
- Has v³, v, x. But x*cos(t) ≠ x*t. Has extra terms v*x², x³, x/(c1+x²). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 46:** `c0*x/(c1+x²) + c2*x³ + c3*x*cos(c4*t) + c5*x + c6*v + c7*x*sin(c8*t + c9)`
- No v³. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 50:** `c0*x/(c1+x²) + c2*v + c3*x*cos(c4*t) + c5*v³ + c6*x³ + c7*x⁵`
- No x·t (x*cos doesn't give x*t), extra terms. **[NO MATCH]**

After checking all candidates: None have the required combination of v³, v, x·t, x, and sin(t) without extra non-eliminable terms.
